#### Opcodes

```
  0: 0x0DE0 [0x42] SET_CLI_EVENT_CANCEL_DATA()
  1: 0x0DE1 [0x43] SEND_EVENT_UPDATE: Send pending tag to server (packet 0x005B)
  2: 0x0DE3 [0x43] SEND_EVENT_UPDATE: Check pending flag (skip if not pending)
  3: 0x0DE5 [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[0] = Work_Zone[9]
  4: 0x0DEA [0x45] LOAD_SCHEDULED_TASK: Load scheduler "fdo1" with entities [EventEntity, EventEntity], work=[200*, 0*]
  5: 0x0DFB [0x55] WAIT_LOAD_SCHEDULER: Wait for scheduler "fdo1" with entities [EventEntity, EventEntity], work=200*
  6: 0x0E0A [0x46] CAMERA_CONTROL: Disable user control
  7: 0x0E0C [0x38] SET_CLIENT_EVENT_MODE(mode=19*)
  8: 0x0E0F [0x4E] SET_ENTITY_HIDE_FLAG: Show LocalPlayer
  9: 0x0E15 [0x34] LOAD_UNLOAD_ZONE(zone_id=50*)
```
